Although the project is dangerous, fortunately there are many people and sufficient materials, so it is not expected to have any accidents. In other places in the lower reaches, the water level rose one Gongcun (unit of length) at Wang Wangzhuang in Putai on the south bank today, and one Gongcun at Scorpion Bay in Bin County. The water level dropped five Gongcun at Dongzhuang in Puyang County on the south bank of the upper reaches, and two Gongcun at Shilibu in Shou Zhang. The construction situation at Zhukou in the upper reaches on the 4th was also relatively stable. In the middle reaches, the water level at Luokou rose one Gongcun and nine Fen (unit of length), with a water level of 30 meters and one inch (90 feet and 3 inches), only 8 inches and 7 Fen lower than the highest water level last year. The River Affairs Bureau is working around the clock. Director Zhang Lianjia only returned to Luokou last night after inspecting the lower reaches. Jinan Mayor Wen Chenglie, considering that Luokou is close to Jinan and of great importance, arrived at Luokou at 4:30 AM this morning to inspect the situation and only returned to Jinan with River Affairs Bureau Director Zhang Lianjia at 7:30 AM. (August 6th)

Wu Tiecheng Proposes Revising the Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law 72

▲ Advocates Restoring Compulsory Arbitration

Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng made a proposal to the Central Political Conference, stating that the Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law abandoned compulsory arbitration and adopted voluntary arbitration, which led to a situation where, when labor-management disputes arise, the government cannot arbitrate unless the parties request arbitration. Furthermore, in the procedures for submitting to arbitration, the government cannot adopt compulsory measures, allowing both labor and management to act as they please, each going to extremes. He specifically described the various facts and reasons and proposed to re-revise the Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law to restore compulsory arbitration, or to allow Shanghai to formulate separate laws and regulations to adopt compulsory arbitration in order to prevent future troubles. This was discussed at the 319th meeting of the Central Political Conference, and it was resolved to restore the compulsory arbitration method and hand it over to the Legislative Yuan for review. On the 6th, the 196th plenary session of the Legislative Yuan resolved to hand it over to the Labor Law Drafting Committee for review. The following is the proposal of Wu:

Since the Shanghai War, the market has been sluggish, and industries have been exhausted. Both labor and management have suffered. Disputes over wages and working hours and dismissals and suspensions have been heard daily. In the past, it started with direct negotiations between labor and management. If the negotiations failed, disputes would arise. If the disputes continued, both sides would go to extremes. The management would deal with the labor by closing factories and shutting down businesses, and the labor would deal with the management by striking and going slow. Both sides confronted each other with direct action, ignoring mediation and arbitration. Although the reasons for this are varied, the abandonment of compulsory arbitration in the Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law and the adoption of voluntary arbitration, which meant that the arbitration award could not bind the parties to the arbitration and that the government and the courts could not enforce the arbitration award, was a major reason for promoting direct action. If we want to reduce factory closures and strikes, we must establish the government's power to resolve labor-management disputes. And if we want the government to establish the power to resolve labor-management disputes, we must adopt compulsory arbitration. Compulsory arbitration contains several characteristics that are sufficient to establish the government's power. According to the current legislative practice, the main points of compulsory arbitration are as follows: (1) If mediation of a labor-management dispute fails, it must be submitted to arbitration. (2) Witnesses must testify and submit documents. (3) Factory closures and strikes are prohibited during mediation, evidence gathering, and adjudication. (4) Arbitration must be adjudicated and announced. (5) The adjudication must be enforced, and no objections may be raised. Factory closures and strikes are prohibited during the effective period, and violators will be fined or imprisoned. China's Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law was promulgated on March 9th of the 17th year (of the Republic) and was scheduled for a one-year trial period. It was extended repeatedly until March of the 19th year, when it was revised by the Legislative Yuan. The first Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law adopted compulsory arbitration, but the revised version changed it to voluntary arbitration. Article 4 of the first Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law stipulates (If a labor-management dispute arises in the following industries, and the mediation of the event is unsuccessful, it shall be submitted to arbitration: (1) Military manufacturing directly operated by military organs; (2) Water, electricity, and gas businesses that supply public needs; (3) Postal, telegraph, telephone, railway, streetcar, shipping, and public automobile businesses that supply public use). Article 5 also stipulates (If the mediation of a labor-management dispute event other than those mentioned in the preceding article is unsuccessful, it shall be submitted to the arbitration committee for arbitration upon the request of both parties to the dispute. However, if the administrative authorities believe that the dispute is of great importance and has been prolonged for more than a month without resolution, and deem it necessary to arbitrate, even without the request of the parties to the dispute, they may submit the dispute to the arbitration committee for arbitration). According to the above two articles, the government may use compulsory means in the procedures for submitting to arbitration. Article 7 stipulates (The parties to the dispute may not object to the arbitration committee's adjudication. The adjudication in the preceding paragraph shall be regarded as a labor contract between the parties to the dispute. If the duration of the arbitration adjudication regarded as a labor contract in the preceding paragraph is expressly stipulated, neither party may, within the said period, propose to change the adjudication, except for lawful termination of the contract). Article 38 stipulates (A party to the dispute who fails to perform the adjudication regarded as a labor contract as stipulated in Article 7, paragraph 2, shall be fined not more than 200 yuan or detained for not more than 40 days. In the case of the preceding paragraph, the party to the dispute may separately request compulsory execution from the court in accordance with civil laws and regulations). The above two articles stipulate the binding force of the arbitration adjudication. This compulsory arbitration has been in effect for two years and has achieved considerable results. Both labor and management believe that the government has the final power to resolve labor-management disputes, and that all labor-management disputes can be resolved after arbitration. Therefore, the management does not have to resort to closing factories and shutting down businesses, and the labor does not have to resort to striking and going slow. Both labor and management benefit from it. However, the revised Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law hastily abandoned compulsory arbitration and adopted voluntary arbitration. The articles on compulsory arbitration in the old law, such as Articles 4, 5, 7, and 38, no longer exist in the new law, and the added articles clearly stipulate that arbitration cannot compel both parties to submit to and execute it. Article 4 of the revised Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law stipulates (When the mediation of a labor-management dispute event is unsuccessful, it shall be submitted to the arbitration committee for arbitration upon the request of both or one of the parties to the dispute). In submitting to arbitration, the government cannot arbitrate if the parties do not request arbitration. Article 5 also stipulates (If a party to a dispute does not object to the arbitration committee's adjudication within five days after the adjudication is served, the adjudication shall be regarded as a contract between the parties to the dispute. If one of the parties to the dispute is a labor union, it shall be regarded as a labor contract between the parties to the dispute). The parties to the dispute may object to the arbitration adjudication within five days. After an objection is raised, the arbitration adjudication has no binding effect on the parties. And the court, based on the party's lawsuit, may overturn the original adjudication and render a new judgment (see Interpretation No. 723 of the Judicial Yuan). This means that the government is not the final authority for handling labor-management disputes and has no actual power to resolve labor-management disputes. And the court may overturn the adjudication jointly adjudicated by its representative (a court representative also attends the arbitration) and the party and government organs and render a new judgment. The same case is handled twice, causing unnecessary disputes. And the case must go through three trials before it can be finalized. The effect is slow and cumbersome, and it is not a good law for handling serious labor-management disputes. Based on the above facts and reasons, it is imperative to re-revise the Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law and restore compulsory arbitration. Otherwise, please allow Shanghai to formulate separate laws and regulations to adopt compulsory arbitration for trial and to prevent hidden dangers. Is this appropriate? I respectfully request a public decision.

Local Communications

Songjiang 73

▲ Director of the Construction Department Inspects the Sea Dike: The Hai Dike in the southern part of this county has been in disrepair for many years and is gradually collapsing. Last autumn, a huge tide flooded the area, nearly causing an accident. Local people have repeatedly requested repairs, but due to the large scale of the project and the high cost, although there are plans, they have not been implemented. This year, Xu Baikui, the director of the Construction Bureau, is actively proceeding with the repairs, uniting all sectors of society to discuss the repairs. The third section of the cement project in Jinshan Mouth and other places in this county is contracted by the Shanghai Construction Factory. Since the start of construction, under the supervision of Director Xu, construction has been carried out quickly and is progressing very rapidly. The completion date is approaching. Dong Xiujia, the director of the Construction Department, attaches great importance to the dike project. He arrived in Songjiang today (the 8th). The Songjiang Steamship of the Bianli Steamship Company, hired by the Construction Bureau, waited for Director Dong at the station. Director Xu greeted him at the station at about 10:00 AM and accompanied him to the bureau. After a brief rest, he accompanied him on the ship and went to inspect the sea dike in Shanyang, Jinshan Mouth, Tuolin, and other places, making a week-long inspection. He will return to Songjiang that evening.

Qingpu 74

▲ A Severe Epidemic in Chonggu Town: Chonggu Town in the ninth district of this county is a prosperous market town with a large population. Since the beginning of summer, the weather has been dry, leading to a widespread epidemic. Patients experience vomiting and diarrhea, and their minds quickly become unclear. Even doctors are at a loss. For example, the housewife of Guangfengyi in the town and Sheng Fuxing of Zhang Gongxing have both died from morning to evening. Currently, twenty to thirty people have died from the epidemic. If no remedies are quickly sought, it is feared that the epidemic will spread further.

Wuxi 75

▲ Requesting the Prohibition of Evil Educational Practices: In this county, before the founding of the Republic, there was a kind of evil practice. Those with a little power in the area could avoid paying silver and grain taxes. After the founding of the Republic, this custom gradually disappeared, but new evil practices have emerged, mostly in rural areas. The children of local thugs and ruffians who go to school often do not pay tuition. If the principal and teachers urge them to pay, they will be angered, or they will collude with accomplices to stir up trouble, create all kinds of rumors, fabricate false accusations, or support unqualified youths to become principals and teachers, misleading students, or establish private schools to hinder the progress of public schools, in order to protect their jobs. Principals and teachers who want to keep their jobs have no choice but to let them not pay and secretly swallow their grievances, watching as public and private interests are jeopardized, and the school spirit deteriorates as a result. The future of the school is also bleak. There is only the name of a school, but no real education. Local enthusiasts, fearing the rampage of these people, mostly sit idly by. Shi Qinglin, Chen Yuanzhu, Hu Xisen, and others in this county cannot bear to see these people destroy this county's education, and they have requested the county government to strictly investigate and prohibit them in order to maintain the school and achieve the popularization of education.

▲ Unscrupulous Merchants Import Inferior Goods: A certain unscrupulous merchant in a certain clothing store on Zhongshi Main Street in the city has recently imported a large number of inferior cloths. This was discovered by the "Blood Soul Extermination Group" of this county, which has sent him a bomb as a serious warning and has also requested the Public Security Bureau not to interfere. It is said that the unscrupulous merchant was quite alarmed after receiving the letter.

▲ Director of the Education Bureau Accused: Sun Xinyuan, the director of the Danyang Education Bureau, has been repeatedly accused. The Education Department has specially sent Provincial Supervisor Feng Ce to Danyang to investigate. It is said that Supervisor Feng is conducting a detailed investigation into the income and expenditure of the bureau's education funds, as well as personnel and administrative issues, and plans to convene the plaintiffs who accused Sun to talk in order to seek a fair resolution.

▲ The Danli Steamer Robbed: The Danli Steamer was sailing near Jintan yesterday when a group of bandits suddenly opened fire and ordered the steamer to stop. They jumped on board and searched and robbed at will. After checking the passengers, it was found that clothing and silver dollars worth about 800 yuan were lost. The case has now been reported to the police for investigation.

Zhenjiang 77

▲The Jiangsu Industrial Bureau Loans Cotton Yarn: Since the disasters in Jiangsu Province, the number of unemployed workers in various places has gradually increased. In Zhenjiang, most of the former cloth factories have now closed. According to a survey by the Industry Bureau, there are more than 100 weaving machines that have stopped operating. In order to provide relief to these unemployed workers, officials were sent to the Dasheng Yarn Factory to negotiate borrowing 50 boxes of yarn to lend to the machine owners to recruit workers and resume production. After they weave the cloth, the yarn cost will be repaid, or the cloth will be used as collateral. It is estimated that it can accommodate more than 200 workers. It is also planned to convene representatives from the Chamber of Commerce, the silk and cloth industry guild, and machine owners to form a Zhenjiang Cotton Weaving Industry Guidance Committee to guide the implementation. If it can be implemented effectively, it will be extended to other places. However, the yarn cost must be repaid three months after the loan is issued. Because the yarn produced by the Dasheng Yarn Factory has already been mortgaged to the banking syndicate, the yarn price still needs to be paid in advance. After consultation with the local Central Bank, it was agreed to use the original 40,000 taels of official shares of the factory in the province to borrow 20,000 yuan in cash for temporary payment of the yarn price. The Dasheng Yarn Factory also specially agreed to reduce the price by 10 yuan per box to pay for bank interest. Now that these shares are under the custody of the Finance Bureau, a special request was made at yesterday's provincial government committee meeting to order the allocation of 40,000 taels of face value for application. After the yarn price is cleared in the future, these shares will be returned in full. The resolution was passed.

Yangzhou 78

▲Water District Five Rescues Two Children: Wu Guangkuan's house, a police officer in the Gua district, was robbed, and two children were kidnapped. They have now been rescued by the head of Water District Five, who dispatched someone to take a night boat to a small boat deep in the reeds about twelve miles from Twelve Forts. The two children were found sleeping soundly in the boat and were immediately rescued and taken to the district, where they were handed over to the victim to file a report and take them back. All the bandits captured in the case have been sent to the Security Department for legal action.

▲The Lianghuai Transportation Office is Ordered to be Abolished: Wang Zhanghu, the Lianghuai Salt Transport Commissioner, was transferred to the Yangzhou Audit Branch as manager according to an order from the Ministry of Finance. The position of Salt Transport Commissioner will be abolished immediately. He is scheduled to come to Yangzhou on the 8th to take over the matter. It is also learned that the Huainan Deputy Transport Office will be merged into the Yangzhou Branch. Hu Xingchi, the Deputy Transport Commissioner, has left Yangzhou today. The current manager of the Yangzhou Branch, Ma Taiwei, will return to the Dongtai Branch after handing over his duties. The former manager, Zhou Sannong, has been ordered to serve as the manager of the Southern Anhui Audit Branch.

Baseball Friendship Match: China Defeats McLing 80

▲China Wins 10 to 7 in the Seventh Inning

▲Wonderful Performance, Extremely Interesting

In the friendly match between the Chinese baseball team and the McLing second team, McLing won the first two times. After this setback, the Chinese team strived to rejuvenate and hoped for a good result. In the third battle yesterday, they finally achieved their wish. The Chinese team won 10 to 7. This is the first masterpiece since the establishment of the Chinese team. All the players were energetic and overjoyed. If this continues, it is very optimistic. The details are recorded as follows:

▲China Gets Off to a Good Start: At 3:30 in the afternoon, the stands of the baseball field were filled with four or five hundred spectators. China started the attack first. Liang Chengson succeeded in one hit, and the ball flew to the center field, reaching third base. Li Beiliang followed. Due to the opponent's mistake, Liang returned to home base, and Li reached second base. Later, two people were killed, but Zhang Zhaoyuan, Liang Fuchu, and Zhang Guoxun still tried to advance, occupying all bases, which was a very good situation. Unexpectedly, when Wei Zongtang hit the ball, the ball was caught by the McLing pitcher and sent to home base. Li Beiliang was blocked. The overall situation changed. Under this situation, China only scored one point, which was a pity. China then changed to defense. McLing batted but did not score anything.

▲McLing's Surprise Attack: In the second inning, China attacked again. An Lesheng entered the field, but the ball was not hit far, but the McLing shortstop made a mistake, and An fortunately reached second base. Jin Zhendong and Li Wenxuan assisted him, and An returned to home base, scoring one point. After the change of lineup, McLing was very aggressive and made continuous hits. Freeman got on base with four balls, and Le Fa hit a long ball, flying over the wire net to the right field, becoming a triple. Freeman then returned to home base. After that, McLing hit every ball, and the momentum was extremely strong. Ma Lun, Boser, and Li successively returned to home base. In total, McLing scored four points, and China fell behind 2 to 4.

▲Masterpiece of the Third Inning: In the top of the third inning, both sides had masterpieces. China attacked first. Liang Fuchu hit a single and reached base, as did Liang Chengson. Wei Zongtang made a sacrifice hit, and Chengson returned quickly, scoring one point. Guoxun crossed to second base, Jin Zhendong hit a long ball, flying to the left field, for a single. Guoxun also returned to home base. Li Wenxuan hit a fastball to the right field, and Jin Zhendong reached third base. Taking advantage of McLing's mistake, he returned to home base. Chengson also got another single, and Li Wenxuan also returned to home base, scoring a total of five points. After the change of lineup, McLing suffered a major setback and launched an active counterattack. Le Fa hit the center field, and the center fielder made a mistake. Nabul and Freeman at second and third bases each returned to home base. Later, Ma Lun hit a single, and Le Fa also returned, scoring three points. In total, the result of the first three innings was a tie of 7 to 7.

▲Zero for Both Sides in the Fourth and Fifth Innings: In the fourth inning, after two Chinese players were killed, they filled the bases with hope, but failed to get a single and gave up. McLing also scored nothing in this inning. China had zero in the fifth inning. McLing attacked hard. China relied on the spirit of individual struggle and killed three people, which was wonderful and easy.

▲China Adds Two More Points: In the top of the sixth inning, Wei Zongtang hit the ball and got on base first. Li Beiliang replaced him as a runner. An Lesheng followed. Although the ball he hit was not very far, he reached second base due to a mistake in the right field. Li Wenxuan tried his best. Li Beiliang ran back and was blocked. Liang Fuchu made a single, and An and Li returned to home base, and Liang reached third base. In the bottom of the inning, McLing was the hitter, but was killed by China in a row, which was extremely fast and wonderful.

▲McLing Fails After Hard Battle: Zhang Zhaoyuan and Zhang Guoxun of China successively reached base. Wei Zongtang once again embraced the principle of sacrifice, gently touched the ball, and Zhang Zhaoyuan returned to home base in a hurry, adding one point. After the change of field, McLing continued to work hard and made a final effort. Although they had advanced to second base, they were eventually killed by China. As a result, China won 10 to 7. In this battle, China made a total of 15 singles, while McLing had 10. McLing made as many as 11 errors, while China had only three. Third Rotary Cup: China Wins the Final Right, British and American Forces Equal

▲Chinese Doubles Wins Again Against Portugal

▲British Doubles Wins Against America, Situation Equal

The singles match between the British and American teams against Portugal was cancelled this afternoon.

In the third Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament, the Chinese doubles defeated Portugal in straight sets yesterday to win the final. At the same time, the British doubles defeated the United States, creating an equal situation. Starting at 4:30 this afternoon, there will be two singles matches between Britain and the United States. The remaining two singles matches between China and Portugal were cancelled with the consent of both parties because the victory was already determined.

(1) China's Invincible Combination Against Portugal 82

Lin Baohua, Jiang Daozhang (China) 6-4, 6-1, 6-4 Cola Sha, Kao Siluan (Portugal)

After Britain's victory over the United States, the audience's emotions were greatly boosted. When the Chinese players Lin Baozhang and Jiang Daozhang strode into the arena, they were greeted with applause. Before long, the Portuguese players also came to the arena. Everyone calmed down and watched the battle.

▲Engraved Articles: In the first set, China and Portugal attacked each other fiercely, neither side yielding. The Lin-Jiang doubles team, known for its fame, also found it difficult to gain an advantage. The strategies of both sides were exactly the same, making great use of sharp serves and waiting for the opponent to counterattack. The other person blocked it and took advantage of the situation to win. Jiang won the first game by relying on this method. Portugal followed suit and succeeded. Thus, the situation of 1-1 to 4-4 was like engraved articles, all the same. In the ninth game, Jiang won again, and in the tenth game, Cola Sha served. At first, he still had the advantage, but Lin's violent shot broke the routine and suddenly changed the situation. As a result, China won 6-4.

▲Head-on Blow: In the second set, the gap between China and Portugal was huge. The former launched a head-on blow, sparing no effort, while the latter was weakened and confused, not knowing what to do. The brilliant masterpiece of one serve and one block seemed to be the exclusive patent of the former. In the second game, Portugal spent all its efforts to win one game, while the rest were won by us. China won again 6-1.

▲The Last Scene: In the third set, the Portuguese side cheered up a bit. At first, they were in a difficult situation, trailing 1-3. When they worked hard, the situation gradually changed. Soon, they saw a 4-4 tie. Lin and Jiang Anken failed in the face of an established situation, intensified their work, and bravely advanced. The last scene was a success. As a result, China won again 6-4.

(2) British Victory Over the United States, Always on Top 83

Hui Te, Turner (England) 6-4, 6-4, 6-3 Shi Kuiya, Bai Lando (America)

On the first day, the United States won the singles against England. Yesterday, England won the doubles against the United States. Each won one group, and the high and low could not be distinguished. Looking at the overall performance of both sides yesterday, the British veteran Hui Te was agile and majestic. Young juniors found it difficult to compete with him. He was the most special person among the four. Shi Kuiya and Turner also had excellent performances. Only Shi's partner, Bai Lando, performed poorly. The failure of the United States lies here. In the first set, Shi opened the serve and won the first game. Hui Te soon regained the second game. Suddenly, after 1-2, England won four consecutive games, and the winning momentum was determined. They finally won 6-4. In the second set, England took the lead and benefited from the transition. The United States tried to catch up, but failed and lost again 4-6. In the third set, the British ball momentum was even stronger, and the United States' efforts were ineffective. In the end, the victory belonged to England with 6-3.

Recent News on the Preparation of the National Sports Association 86

▲Chen Shizhen and Zhong Lingxiu are additionally hired as committee members

▲91 members from 19 provinces and cities have registered

The National Sports Conference is scheduled to be held at the Nanjing Lizhi Society starting on the 16th of this month. The conference period was originally set for July. In the future, depending on the number of motions, it may be extended by a few days, which is still difficult to determine. Generally, during the conference, there will be a general meeting in the morning and review meetings and group meetings in the afternoon. The preparatory committee of the association originally hired Chu Minyi, Zhang Zhijiang, Zhou Yawei, Wu Yunrui, Huang Mingdao, Guo Xinsong, Gu Shusen, Li Zheng, Peng Baichuan and other nine people. Now, Chen Shizhen and Zhong Lingxiu have been additionally hired, for a total of eleven people. (In fact, there are still nine people because Guo Xinsong, the Director of Higher Education, is on leave, and is currently being replaced by Chen Shizhen, a counselor. Li Zheng, the Director of Social Education, has gone to the Beijing Normal University and is temporarily being concurrently handled by Zhong Lingxiu, the section chief.) The association expects more than 100 members to attend the meeting. A check as of the 6th shows that the members who have sent letters to participate and have designated representatives include 11 preparatory committee members, 22 experts invited from various places, 3 scheme formulation committee members, and representatives from various agencies (such as the Ministry of Interior, Railways, Industry, Communications, Training General Supervision, Chinese Boy Scout Command, etc.), representatives from the Education Departments and Bureaus of various provinces and cities, representatives from national martial arts halls, and directors of physical education from colleges and universities. The total is 55 people. The above statistics are 91 people (excluding the employees and secretaries of the Ministry of Education). Except for Rehe, which has sent a letter stating that it will not send representatives due to special circumstances, Liangdu, Xinjiang, Sichuan, and the three northeastern provinces have not yet sent letters informing them of the representatives who will attend the meeting. The provinces and cities that have reported and designated representatives are Jiangsu, Nanjing, Shanghai, Qinghai, Chahar, Yunnan, Gansu, Fujian, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Hubei, Qingdao, Anhui, Guizhou, Henan, Shandong, Shaanxi, Hebei, and Suiyuan, and other 19 provinces and cities. The Ministry of Education previously issued an order to the Education Departments and Bureaus of various provinces and cities, requesting them to forward it to the provincial, municipal, and registered private universities or independent colleges, and various physical education specialty schools to comply with the provisions of Article 2, and quickly select the members who should be sent, and submit their names and resumes to the Ministry of Education before August 1. On the 6th, the Ministry of Education received letters from two universities in a certain city stating that they had not received notification from the city bureau. The Ministry of Education has ordered the city bureau to investigate and supplement the notification. For any province or city with the same omission, it is hoped that they will make up for it as soon as possible due to the approaching conference period, so as not to delay the matter. In order to promote the use of domestic sports equipment, the association has had the Shanghai Standard Sports Equipment Company transport more than 200 kinds of domestic sports equipment to be displayed at the conference. If there are other domestic sports equipment companies with equipment to display, they can directly contact the association.

Local News

Recent News from the Wusong Merchant Marine School 97

The Wusong Merchant Marine School, under the Ministry of Communications, reopened on May 28th after Xia Sunpeng was appointed as the principal by the Ministry of Communications in May. There are over two hundred students. Its funding comes from one-third of the import ship taxes, allocated to the school and managed by a specially formed management committee. The entire faculty consists of about forty members. Since the outbreak of the war, the salaries for March, April, and May have not been paid. The faculty has repeatedly requested payment since the reopening, but without success. In July, the faculty formed a union and demanded their salaries from the principal. Xia Sunpeng forwarded the request to the Ministry of Communications, which ruled that the salaries for March and April would not be paid as they were during the school closure period. The faculty held a second general meeting and resolved: (1) to request the Ministry to first pay the May salaries; (2) if the salaries for March and April were not resolved by the end of July, they would go on strike on August 1st. At the same time, faculty members Meng Xian, Wang Gui, Sun Xudaqing, and others were chosen to meet with the principal, who would forward the request to the Ministry. Fearing a strike on August 1st, the Ministry first issued a reply through the Navigation Administration Department, earnestly advising everyone to consider the overall situation, postpone the strike temporarily, and await the Ministry's review and approval of a plan for compliance. The faculty has patiently waited, but has not yet received a reply.

Moths Around the Gauze Lamp Shade 100

— Zhan Lu

Gauze lamp shade! Gauze lamp shade! Many moths are hovering and circling around you! In summer, to isolate flies from food, it is necessary to add a gauze cover; especially for cooked meat, the aroma of meat is overflowing, which has a special magic power to attract flies. The gauze cover on cooked meat is necessary among the necessary.

The foolish flies are coming! There is a target inside the gauze cover. You can see it, and you can smell it, but you just can't satisfy the physiological requirements of the flies. Except hovering and circling around the gauze cover, there is no other way.

Is this the temptation of meat? No, this is the unrequited love of flies, not the temptation of meat. A bowl of cooked meat inside the gauze cover has no consciousness and will not move by itself; even if the foolish flies unrequitedly love to death, it is the fault of the foolish flies and not the fault of the meat.

In the park, under the green shade, by the evening breeze, there are many spirits and flesh moving inside the gauze cover! This gauze cover is not an iron gauze cover, but a georgette shirt that fully reveals the skin.

The foolish flies are coming! There is a target inside the gauze cover. You can see it, and you can smell it, and maybe you can satisfy the physiological requirements of the flies. Therefore, the flies are buzzing and saying: I linger for a long time, I can't bear to leave.

Is this the unrequited love of flies? No, this is the temptation of the flesh, not the unrequited love of flies. The spirit and flesh inside the georgette gauze cover are conscious and will move by themselves. In the park, under the green shade, by the evening breeze, the flesh is sending out invitations to the flies.

Despicable flesh! Poor foolish flies!

The Life of Great Figures 101

— Qian

I have a friend. He graduated from Huangpu Military Academy. I have been separated from him for several years. One day, I accidentally met him in Shanghai. It turns out that he is now serving as a military instructor at a certain university.

I said, (You have been out of touch since you graduated from military school. You have had a lot of experience in these few years.)

He said, (I have had a lot of experience in these years. I have been to Beijing, Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Guiyang, Chengdu, Wuhan, and other places. But my experience has made me very disheartened. Let me tell you simply.

(After I graduated, I was assigned to a certain division as a trainee, first as a platoon leader, and later promoted to company commander. Although I was only a junior officer, I was very satisfied with my life at this time.

(Later, due to changes in the environment, I also left a certain division and ran around. As a result, unexpectedly, I became the director of the anti-smoking bureau of a certain county in Hubei. I don't like money. But at this time, there was so much money. Three or five thousand a month is simply nothing. My subordinates would stuff thousands into their pockets every month. Besides, there were more than a dozen friends gathered around you. Clothing, food, pocket money, everything must be supplied by you. I really hated this kind of life. I said, okay, let you do it. So soon I resigned from my position.

After I resigned, I went to several places. Later, I became a liaison staff officer of a certain division. The liaison staff officer is responsible for the liaison between the military divisions. The position is very high. When you go to the division headquarters, you are at the same level as the division commander. When you go to the military headquarters, you are at the same level as the military commander. The salary is also very generous. But even though there is a lot of money, you can't save a penny. Why? Because I am a liaison staff officer, I have to socialize. Otherwise, I can't get in touch. And the worst thing in the army is that you can't socialize without (mahjong). Alas. When I think of my life at this time, I really feel sad. When I wake up in the morning, the affairs are very clear. But when I want to read a book, someone comes. They don't come to deliver any official business. It's just that A asks you to find a job. B asks you to intercede. C asks you to do sports. D comes to chat with you. A day's work is spent on these trivial matters. At four o'clock in the afternoon, a call comes from a certain military headquarters. A call comes from a certain division headquarters. Go to a certain hotel to open a room. Go to a certain hotel to play mahjong. You have to go. And the people who play mahjong with me have their names in the newspapers. Military commander. Division commander. Chief of staff. They are all big figures. And playing cards in the army is different from ordinary playing cards. The winnings and losses are not thirty or fifty. At least three hundred or five hundred. Do you think I can get along with them? From this, I came to a conclusion. That is, great figures live a (non-human life). I really hated it. I thought, (I'd better go back). So soon I resigned and came to a certain university as a military instructor through a friend's introduction. Of course, the salary is not as much as it was then. But there is no socializing and no trouble. My heart is much clearer.)

The Tragedy of the Fierce Fight between the Two Associations 103

— Li Hongbin

My friend Mr. Li is from Shandong and serves as a soldier in Sichuan. In the spring of the seventeenth year, he returned to his hometown due to an event. He passed through Zhangde, Henan on the way. As it was getting dark, he stayed at a small inn in Wuyi Village. There were already three travelers there. He went to bed at midnight, but he had not yet fallen asleep. Suddenly, he heard a noisy human voice. He couldn't distinguish what they were saying. He was startled and looked up, but he saw dozens of people gathering and talking, looking very angry. He asked the innkeeper. He said, "Guests are from faraway villages, so it doesn't matter if I tell you. But be careful not to leak it out. I'm afraid it will be unfavorable to everyone. There are about five hundred households in our village, which are divided into the Tianmen and Red Spear Associations. I belong to the Tianmen Association. Whenever something happens in the village, the leaders of the two associations discuss it before acting. They respect each other and there have never been any conflicts. However, three days ago, twelve deserters entered the village with guns and horses, acting violently. They could not be reasoned with. The two associations jointly killed them. Afterwards, the Tianmen Association planned to get their guns, while the Red Spear Association would get their horses. The Red Spear Association insisted on half of the guns and horses. They discussed for three days but could not decide. Now they have broken up and are preparing for war. We are members of the association, so we should go through the number. Unfortunately, you have also encountered this robbery. Only you." Mr. Li argued, "Then can we avoid it?" The innkeeper said, "It is impossible to escape. At this time, spies are lurking everywhere. No one can cross the Leichi pool. However, I will do my best to help you plan it." So he went to tell the leaders of the two associations. The leaders of the associations agreed to it. So each association sent someone to send them out with lanterns and weapons. After passing through Gang Kafa, they all said that they were ordered to send guests. They checked carefully and then let them go. When they were half a mile away from the village, the sender said, "You

should go quickly. There will be no obstacles in the future."

A month later, Mr. Li finished his work and went to Sichuan. He passed through the village again. He arrived at the small inn. The door was deserted and there was no human voice. He entered the house. Only an old woman was cooking by the stove. Mr. Li said his intention and asked about the innkeeper. The old woman suddenly burst into tears and said, "About three hours after you left that night, the war broke out. As a result, the Tianmen Association was defeated. My husband and three sons and two daughters-in-law all died. The family was broken and destroyed.

Business has been suspended for a long time. I can't accommodate distinguished guests." Mr. Li sighed and walked out. The sound of sobbing has not yet stopped. Alas, what a tragedy.

Love Doesn't Forget to Save the Country 104

— Ying

(Saving the country doesn't forget love. Love doesn't forget saving the country.) This is a paraphrase of (saving the country doesn't forget reading. Reading doesn't forget saving the country.) This is the fashionable talk of a group of young men and women. On the surface, it seems that the meaning of the two sentences is the same. In fact, when the words change, the meaning is very different. Because the previous sentence (saving the country doesn't forget love.) has to save the country and still can't forget love. It is in line with the old saying (heroes are short of breath. Children's love is long.) As a result, his (her) work of saving the country. Did not succeed. I am afraid it will also be a failure. The next sentence (love doesn't forget saving the country.) He (she) can wake up from the maze of love. Go to save the country. He (she) must understand that love is narrow love. Saving the country is broad love. How great this kind of thinking is.

Recently, Tianyi Company produced a sound film (Two Orphans in the Battlefield.) It is to elaborate on the meaning of (love does not forget to save the country). Two women. In the midst of chaos and displacement. Love the same man. Due to various environmental factors. Almost caused a love triangle tragedy. But as a result, she and he both abandoned their private love. Go to the national crisis together. The story has many twists and turns. Extremely happy and sad. The content is tragic and exciting. It is inspiring and exciting. Young men and women who like to talk about love now. It is necessary to watch this film.

National Goods Factories Worth Introducing (20) 105

— He Gongxing

(31) Brick and Tile Factory

Since French Red Ping Chain-style tiles were imported into China, our country's old green clay bricks and tiles have been almost eliminated. Therefore, we had to adapt to the changes of the times and imitate them. New-style bricks and tiles have emerged as the times require.

In the early years of the Republic of China, Zhu Zhiyao, a Shanghai merchant, founded a kiln factory in Sanlintang, Pudong. He built German-style kilns and imitated bricks and tiles. Although it failed soon, it was the beginning of Shanghai's mechanized brick and tile manufacturing. Afterwards, there were Ruihe Brick and Tile Company in Xiaoshadu, Guanghua Pattern Brick Factory in Yongxing Road, Huada Brick and Tile Factory in Beixinjing, Fuji Porcelain Company, Taishan Brick and Tile Company No. 2 Factory in Xinlonghua, Xinda Kiln Factory in Tangwan, and Yizhong Ceramic Tile Factory in Pudong. Dazhong Brick and Tile Factory. Other factories such as Fakang Zhonghe Xiechang Hezhong Xingye, etc., either produce red tiles and green tiles, or produce road bricks and fire bricks, or produce mosaic ceramic tiles. Mosaic is especially a necessity of the times. Fuji and Yizhong products are better and sell well for a while.

Foreigners have established brick and tile factories in Shanghai, including the Yipin Factory opened by Belgian merchants, and the China Cement Brick and Tile Company opened by British merchants. Cement bricks and tiles are strong, light, and sponge-like in shape. They are especially suitable for building high-rise buildings. Unfortunately, their processes and materials are kept strictly confidential and cannot be investigated. I sincerely hope that those who study the brick and tile industry will pay attention to it.

The raw materials for mechanized bricks and tiles are five kinds of yellow mud, ore mud, cement, coal slag, porcelain clay. The products are green tiles, red tiles, red bricks, patterned bricks, road bricks, fire bricks, ceramic tiles, facing bricks, cylinder bricks, hollow bricks, coal slag bricks, and mosaic. The length of the bricks and the size of the price are not uniform. Sales are mostly in this port. Hankou, Nanjing, and Tianjin are second. In recent years, the construction industry has made great progress. This industry is booming. Although Japanese bricks and tiles are not as good as national goods in terms of workmanship and materials, they are sometimes found on the market. The general public does not know the pros and cons and buys them. Shanghai has a Shandong Kiln Industry Company, which is the Japanese brick and tile management office. (End)

Mr. Zhu said: (There are many more amazing facts. There are about seven million students in public and private primary schools across the country: there are at least seven million students in old-style private schools. The total cost of these 14 million primary school students is at least 100 million yuan per year. This 100 million yuan is completely consumed under traditional education. Primary school students are too young, so they cannot fully produce, but raising a few chickens, planting a few vegetables, planting a few trees, and spinning a few kilograms of yarn should not be considered excessive. Otherwise, sweeping and wiping the table and washing their own clothes will save adults a lot of energy and move it to production. The creation of the Republic of China cannot be without these small workers. Look at the financial report from July 1, 1929 to June 30, 1930. The national treasury expenditure in this year was 49,507,000 yuan, of which 49.6% was military expenditure, which is 24,544,000 yuan. This 24,544,000 yuan is spent on military affairs every year, and if it continues to be spent for ten years, it will be 245,440,000 yuan. This sum of money is not only purely consumption but also destroys production. According to the statistics in September of the nineteenth year, there were 2,599,200 formal troops in the country, not including informal troops. Most of these two million five hundred and ninety-nine thousand people are farmers, who could originally produce, but as soon as they enter the army, they immediately become consumers. More soldiers cannot resist foreign insults, and there will inevitably be internal strife. Once internal strife comes, workers cannot do me, farmers cannot cultivate the land, and productivity is destroyed again. The country's raising of soldiers is like hiring a bodyguard. Hiring a bodyguard is only the business of the rich. The poor can only protect themselves, so how can they afford to hire a bodyguard. China is a poor country, and it is impossible to afford to feed soldiers who eat by being soldiers. If we can use this 245 million yuan of military expenditure as production capital and turn these 2.6 million soldiers into productive workers, then what a great construction power it would be!)

Finance The Gold Market Fluctuated Slightly Last Week 108

Both Sides Were in a Standoff

Down Four Taels from the Previous Week

Last week, the gold market benchmark price saw slight changes, appearing to hover, but without any major disturbances. The daily difference was at most six taels. Both the long and short positions were relatively balanced. Initially, the silver market's reported gains slightly weakened, with the opening price for September at 745.5 taels, down eight qian. Subsequently, both silver prices and exchange rates rose. However, Shanghai's exchange rates moved in the opposite direction, becoming strained. With the addition of Guangbang Hengxing and others covering their short positions, it seemed like an upward trend was developing. However, sellers remained active, and the price fluctuated uncertainly, creating a volatile situation. On Tuesday, the price rose to 746.2 qian. By Friday, the situation changed dramatically, and the market almost saw a sharp decline, mainly due to the steep fall in exchange rates. This affected the first order delivery significantly, and the U.S. dollar exchange rate also showed signs of easing. Selling pressure increased in the market, and prices plummeted to 735.6 qian. Although the silver market rose on Saturday, exchange rates continued to fall sharply by three fen, reaching 2.75 fen. However, the U.S. dollar exchange rate surged, reversing the trend from the previous day, rising above 740 taels, eventually reaching 42.3 qian (the grey market price even reached 43.5 qian). Comparing the opening and closing prices of this week, there was a drop of 3.2 qian, with a range of 11.6 qian. Compared to the end of the previous week, the overall drop was 4 taels. As for the British and American silver markets, they continued to rise, leading to an increase of two gears in the local British gold exchange rate (half a penny), while the U.S. dollar only increased by .375. The domestic British gold rose by .375, while the U.S. dollar only recovered by .125, mainly due to the sharp fall in exchange rates. Gold firms mostly sold, while arbitrage transactions were done, but the prices were somewhat far apart. For near-term delivery, it was above 50 taels, and for long-term delivery, it was about 40 taels. Various firms were shorting 4-5 million U.S. dollars, with the initial settlement price at over 70 taels, eventually falling to over 60 taels. The British and American exchange rates initially rose repeatedly, but then fell frequently. The total fall of the British pound against the U.S. dollar was 3.875, and the overall decline of the U.S. dollar was more than four fen. Spot gold is now being gradually absorbed by the Central Bank, or those engaging in arbitrage with U.S. dollars are adding 8-9 taels based on the actual cost. It is also found that the recent volume of gold transactions is approximately 22,000 contracts, with Yuanxingyong still holding the majority of long positions, accounting for about 4,400 contracts, standing in contrast to the short positions held by Hengxing. Run Chang Yu Yifeng Yong only have slightly more than 1,000 contracts, Qianchangxiang about 2,000, Yuandayong only a few hundred, while Zhaofengchang is short 1,500-1,600 contracts. Dadecheng Yifeng and others also hold short positions. The Dalian Gang is slightly long, but the number of contracts held by each firm has decreased compared to the previous week, as the public bonds for August have already been settled. The general situation of the past week is summarized below:

▲Monday: Due to the bank summer vacation, gold transactions were suspended. However, there was no change in the information from the London telegraph. The U.S. silver market also did not fluctuate. Exchange rates returned to .375.

▲Tuesday: No news from the London telegraph, the U.S. silver market rose .125, while HSBC's listed price remained unchanged. The domestic market trended weaker. As for the gold market, it was business as usual. The opening price fell by eight qian, to 745.5 taels. Subsequently, due to buying activity, it rose to 46.2 qian. Afterwards, the exchange market weakened, and selling pressure increased. The price fell to 40 taels, then to 41 taels. The afternoon closing price was 40.02 qian. The afternoon opening price was 40 taels. Later, Hengxing repeatedly bought in, pushing the price to 42.8 qian. The closing price was 42 qian, continuing to fall 400,003 qian compared to the previous Saturday. The highest price of the day was 46.2 qian, and the lowest was 40 taels, a difference of 6.2 qian. Public bonds were settled as usual today (August spot), totaling 5,600 contracts. It was also reported that Shoufengyong settled 4,900 contracts with the Central Bank.

▲Wednesday: The London telegraph rose .0625 repeatedly, the U.S. silver market rose .125, the first order delivery remained unchanged, and the U.S. dollar was listed up .125, as exchange rates had been rising for three days. However, the internal market seemed tight, with a clear divergence between the official and unofficial markets. The gold market opened slightly lower by two qian, at 41.8 qian. Hengxing was the first to take action and buy, followed by 1.6 qian. Subsequently, the market rose by three taels, as there were many buyers, reaching 44.8 qian. Then, due to the exchange market weakening, it fell to 41.7 qian at noon. Eventually, it rose, with buyers remaining active and the exchange market improving, reaching 45 taels. It then closed at 44.8 qian, a rebound of 2.8 qian compared to the previous day. The daily fluctuation was only 3-4 taels, with a maximum of 45 taels and a minimum of 41.6 qian. The afternoon was closed for rest due to the heat.

▲Thursday: The London telegraph fell back .0625, and the U.S. silver market fell .125, a reversal after several days of rising. The first order delivery remained unchanged, while the U.S. dollar decreased by .125. The internal market was calm, as the exchange rate did not move. The gold market opened lower by 2.4 qian, at 42.4 qian. This was due to a surprising surge in New York stock prices, and the forward silver price also rose, leading to fatigue in the market. Subsequently, buyers became active, with Guangbang and Hengxing Yuanlu and others strongly covering their short positions, reaching 45.5 qian at noon and closing at 4 liang. The afternoon opened at 4 liang, then remained very stable, fluctuating by only 7 qian. The closing price was 43.5 qian, down 1.3 qian from the previous day. The daily fluctuation was 5.5 qian at most and 1.5 qian at least, with a difference of 4 liang.

▲Friday: The London telegraph and silver prices remained unchanged. The first order delivery was fearfully set at .25, and the U.S. dollar rose .25, due to the sharp fall in exchange rates. The internal market also weakened. The gold market opened slightly higher by 3 qian, at 43.8 qian, then rose to 4 liang. Subsequently, selling pressure spread, falling to 40.09 qian. Later, the Central Bank absorbed cash, pushing the price to 42.6 qian. However, the selling position remained excessive, breaking through 40 taels at noon, reaching 39 taels, with a closing price of 9.4 qian. The afternoon opened at 7.8 qian, continuing the downward momentum from the noon closing. Then, Hengxing and others bought in, reaching 8.4 qian. However, the situation deteriorated on all sides, eventually falling to 35.6 qian (the lowest price since the swap), with a closing price of 36.5 qian, a sharp drop of 7 taels compared to the previous day. The daily fluctuation was 44 taels at most and 35.6 qian at least, with a difference of 8.4 qian.

▲Saturday: The London telegraph and silver prices both rose by .25. The first order delivery rose by .25, while the U.S. dollar only increased by .125, due to the sharp fall in exchange rates. Therefore, there was a divergence between the internal British and U.S. markets. The gold market initially opened at 37.2 taels, a rebound of 7 qian. Private telegraphs only increased by .0625. From 7.7 qian to 6.7 qian, the Dalian Gang was the first to sell off. Afterwards, buyers became active, and short positions were quickly covered. The exchange market improved, leading to an upward trend. It was rumored that the Central Bank was again absorbing cash, boosting market sentiment. The price moved forward and went past 40 taels. The closing price was 42.3 qian, up 5.8 qian from the previous day. The highest price was 42.4 qian, and the lowest was 36.7 qian, a difference of 5.7 qian. Securities The Bond Market Was Stable and Quiet Last Week 110

▲Increased by More Than One Yuan, with a Transaction Volume of 14 Million

During the past week (from August 1st to August 6th), the local Shanghai Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange continued to operate two trading sessions in the morning. The market was deserted, and trading was extremely rare. Spot transactions totaled only 87,000 yuan for the entire week. Excluding the unified tax of 31,000 yuan, the salt tax of 21,000 yuan, and the 20 Customs Duty of 12,000 yuan, the remaining amount was only a few thousand yuan. There was no trading in the 19 Customs Duty, Charity 96, etc. Although the September futures had been open for bidding for several days, there were often no transactions. Therefore, almost the entire market was dominated by the August futures. The daily transaction volume was only a few hundred thousand yuan, totaling 14,458,000 yuan, a decrease of more than 4.6 million yuan compared to the previous week. This includes 3,055,000 yuan in salt tax, 2,100,000 yuan in disbandment bonds, 2,185,000 yuan in unified tax, 1,620,000 yuan in the 20 issue, 1,595,000 yuan in the 20 Customs Duty, 1,365,000 yuan in the 19 Customs Duty, 1,020,000 yuan in the 19 Charity, and others even less. For example, 815,000 yuan in the Disbandment Bond, 220,000 yuan in Customs Duty, 215,000 yuan in the Restructuring 6 li, 60,000 yuan in the 96 public bonds, and 20,000 yuan in financial bonds. Among these, the September futures for various bonds totaled only 65,000 yuan. As for the changes, the market had fallen sharply in the previous week. Although there were absolutely no turnaround signs in the market last week, it was generally stable. Retail investors bought in at lower prices, and prices rebounded consistently. From Monday to Thursday, prices fluctuated upward every day. However, on the weekend, buying decreased again, and prices weakened again. The entire process of change was very peaceful. Major investors remained on the sidelines, and the market only saw sporadic trading. As a result, compared to the previous week, except for a few spot prices that still fell, other prices rebounded by .56 jiao to 1.5 yuan. In the current market environment, large increases or decreases in the bond market seem unlikely. Therefore, unless there are major changes in the political situation or diplomacy, or significant improvements in the financial situation, the bond market will temporarily be stagnant and difficult to experience large fluctuations. Yarn Market Standard Yarn Fell at the Beginning of the Week, Rebounded at the End 111

Only 3,942 Bales of Current Yarn Were Sold to Customers

At the beginning of the past week, cotton yarn experienced a period of quiet after a large demand from various groups in the southern ports. Generally, it was believed that the current yarn market was sluggish, the war clouds in the Northeast were spreading, and the Tianjin factory yarn was affected by Japanese yarn, leading to blocked sales channels. There were rampant rumors of selling yarn in Shanghai. Sellers actively sold off, and the market price showed a downward trend. However, the Rongxing buyers realized that the factories had depleted their inventories. After selling all the yarn from the factories, the financial situation became much looser. The factories had a positive attitude, and the Yangtze River basin was expected to have a good harvest this year, leading to a strong desire to go long. Therefore, despite a large number of sales, they were absorbed by buyers. Both long and short positions had considerable strength. At the weekend, rumors of 1,500 bales of Tianjin yarn, and all the Hwasing factory's engineering branch yarn were bought by Sichuan buyers. At the same time, the market situation of American cotton and certain foreign yarn was firm, and market sentiment was shaken again, leading to a rise in the market. On the whole, cotton yarn may have a stabilizing possibility. Customer purchases during this week totaled only 3,492 bales, and the market was softening. Sichuan buyers purchased more than 2,000 bales, the most of any group. Others were very small. The standard yarn fell by 2-3 liang at the beginning of the week, and rebounded by more than 2 liang at the end of the week. The total transaction volume for the entire week was 153,950 bales.
